Digital Transformation Management Platform (DTMP v3) Development Prompt

Create a professional internal Digital Transformation Management Platform (DTMP v3) with an internally-focused landing page and marketplaces overview.

# PROJECT CONTEXT

This is **Prompt 1 of 9** in building the complete DTMP v3 platform.

**Key Context:**

* This is an **INTERNAL platform** used by a Transformation Office within an organization
* Audience: Internal stakeholders (TO members, architects, project teams, operations)
* Tone: Operational and governance-focused, not marketing/sales
* Purpose: Orchestrate enterprise-wide digital transformation toward a Digital Business Platform (DBP)

**Building in this prompt:**

* Design system and reusable components
* Header/Navigation (sticky, internal platform style)
* Footer (internal links and resources)
* Landing Page (internal transformation office narrative)
* Marketplace of Marketplaces page (7 marketplaces overview)
* Routing foundation
* Responsive mobile-first design

**NOT building yet:**

* Individual marketplace pages (Prompts 2-8)
* Login modal (Prompt 2)
* Detail pages (Prompts 2-8)
* Stage 2 placeholder (Prompt 2)

## TECHNICAL STACK

* **Framework:** React with TypeScript
* **Routing:** React Router v6
* **Styling:** Tailwind CSS
* **Icons:** Lucide React
* **Responsive:** Mobile-first (breakpoints: 640px, 768px, 1024px, 1280px)

## DESIGN SYSTEM

**Colors (Internal Platform Theme)**

JavaScript

const colors = {

primary: {

navy: '#001F3F', // Dark blue for headers, footers, titles

blue: '#0066CC', // Links and accents

lightBlue: '#E6F2FF', // Card backgrounds, section backgrounds

},

accent: {

orange: '#FF6600', // Primary buttons and key CTAs

purple: '#8B5CF6', // Icons and badges

pink: '#EC4899', // Icons and accents

green: '#10B981', // Success states, checkmarks

},

neutral: {

white: '#FFFFFF',

gray50: '#F9FAFB',

gray100: '#F3F4F6',

gray200: '#E5E7EB',

gray400: '#9CA3AF',

gray600: '#666666', // Secondary text

gray700: '#374151',

gray900: '#111827',

}

}

**Usage:**

* Headers/Footers: Navy (#001F3F) background, white text
* Primary CTAs: Orange (#FF6600) background, white text
* Secondary CTAs: Orange border, orange text, white background
* Cards: White or light blue (#E6F2FF) backgrounds
* Icons: Purple (#8B5CF6), Pink (#EC4899), Orange, Green
* Body text: Gray (#666666) for secondary, gray-900 for primary
* Section backgrounds: Alternate white and light blue

**Typography**

* **Font:** Inter or system sans-serif
* **Headings:** Bold weight (font-bold)
* **Hero Title:** 36-48px (responsive)
* **Section Titles:** 28-36px (responsive)
* **Card Titles:** 18-24px
* **Body:** 16-18px
* **Small text/labels:** 12-14px

**Spacing & Layout**

* **Container:** max-w-7xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8
* **Section Padding:** py-12 (mobile) â†’ py-16 (tablet) â†’ py-20 (desktop)
* **Card Padding:** p-6
* **Grid Gaps:** gap-6 lg:gap-8
* **Border Radius:** rounded-xl (12px) for cards, rounded-lg (8px) for buttons

**Component Patterns**

**Cards:**

* Background: bg-white or bg-blue-50
* Border: border border-gray-200 (subtle, not heavy)
* Rounded: rounded-xl
* Shadow: shadow-sm hover:shadow-lg
* Padding: p-6

**Buttons:**

* Primary: bg-orange-600 text-white hover:bg-orange-700 px-6 py-3 rounded-lg font-semibold
* Secondary: border-2 border-orange-600 text-orange-600 hover:bg-orange-50 px-6 py-3 rounded-lg font-semibold
* With icon: "Text +" (plus sign indicates action)

**Badges:**

* Phase badges (4D):
  + Discern: bg-blue-100 text-blue-700
  + Design: bg-purple-100 text-purple-700
  + Deploy: bg-green-100 text-green-700
  + Drive: bg-orange-100 text-orange-700
* Small: px-3 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold uppercase

**Icons:**

* Colorful, rounded style (use Lucide React)
* Size: 40-48px for section icons, 20-24px for inline
* Colors: purple, pink, orange, blue (varied for visual interest)

* Mobile: < 640px
* Tablet: 640px - 1023px
* Desktop: â‰¥ 1024px

* Mobile: Smaller text, stacked CTAs, quick links in 2x2 grid

* Mobile: Single column, vertical timeline
* Tablet: 2 columns

* Mobile: Single column

* Mobile: Single column
* Tablet: 2 columns
* Desktop: 3 columns

* Desktop: 4 columns

## INTERACTION & ANIMATION PATTERNS

Hover Effects Cards:

CSS

transition: all 0.3s ease

hover: shadow-xl, -translate-y-2, border-orange-500

Buttons:

CSS

transition: all 0.2s ease

hover: background darker shade

active: scale-95

Links:

CSS

transition: color 0.2s ease

hover: text-orange-600

**Smooth Scrolling**

* Enable smooth scroll behavior for anchor links
* Subtle fade-in for sections as they enter viewport (optional)

## ACCESSIBILITY REQUIREMENTS

* All images/icons have aria-labels
* All interactive elements keyboard-navigable
* Focus states visible (ring-2 ring-orange-500)
* Semantic HTML (nav, main, section, article)
* Color contrast meets WCAA standards (test navy text on white, white text on navy)
* Alt text for all graphics

## PLACEHOLDER IMAGES

* Hero: No image needed (gradient background sufficient)
* Icons: Use Lucide React icons as specified
* Marketplace icons: Colorful rounded icon backgrounds with Lucide icons
* No photo placeholders needed

## BUILD SEQUENCE

1. Set up routing and navigation structure
2. Build Header and Footer (reusable, internal platform style)
3. Build Landing Page section by section:
   * Hero with Target State badge
   * DBP Overview
   * 4D Governance Model
   * Execution Streams
   * Resource Marketplaces
   * TO Value
   * Contributors
   * Final CTA
4. Build Marketplaces Page with all 9 marketplace cards
5. Ensure all navigation flows correctly
6. Test responsive behavior thoroughly

Success Criteria:

* Internal platform aesthetic (navy, orange, operational tone)
* User can navigate Home â†’ Marketplaces â†’ Individual marketplace (Coming Soon)
* All sections complete, responsive, and on-brand
* 4D Model, Execution Streams, and Contributors sections clearly communicate internal governance
* 9 marketplaces integrated into Resource Marketplaces section and Marketplaces page
* Platform feels like an internal transformation office tool, not external marketing

Build a professional, internally-focused transformation platform foundation that establishes the governance narrative and operational context for all subsequent marketplace builds.

* Placeholder changes per tab

**DETAIL HEADER**

HTML

<section className="detail-header">

{provider && (

<div className="provider-info">

<span className="attribution">Provided by</span>

<strong className="provider-name">{provider.name}</strong>

</div>

)}

<h1 className="detail-title">{title}</h1>

<div className="badges">

<span className="badge badge-level">{level}</span>

<span className="badge badge-category">{category}</span>

{certification && (

<span className="badge badge-cert">

<Icon name="Award" size={14} />

Certification Available

</span>

)}

</div>

{rating && (

<div className="rating-display">

<div className="stars-large">

{[...Array(5)].map((\_, i) => (

<Icon name={i < Math.floor(rating) ? "Star" : "StarHalf"} size={20} />

))}

</div>

<span className="rating-text-large">

{rating} ({students} students)

</span>

</div>

)}

</section>

**Styling:**

* Padding: py-8 lg:py-12
* Container: max-w-7xl mx-auto px-4
* Provider info: flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-gray-600 mb-4
* Attribution: text-gray-500
* Provider name: text-gray-900
* Detail title: text-3xl lg:text-4xl font-bold text-[#001F3F] mb-4
* Badges: flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-4
* Badge: px-3 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-semibold
  + Level: bg-blue-100 text-blue-700
  + Category: bg-purple-100 text-purple-700
  + Cert: bg-green-100 text-green-700 flex items-center gap-1
* Rating display: flex items-center gap-3
* Stars large: flex gap-1 text-yellow-400 fill-yellow-400
* Rating text large: text-base text-gray-700 font-medium

<span>â€¢</span>

<span>{course.level}</span>

</div>

* Related card title: text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-2 line-clamp-2
* Related desc: text-sm text-gray-600 mb-3 line-clamp-2
* Related meta: flex items-center gap-2 text-xs text-gray-500

**Related Courses Logic:**

* Show 3 courses from same category or same level
* Exclude current course
* Randomize if more than 3 available

**LOGIN MODAL COMPONENT**

**Triggered when:** User clicks "Enroll Now" (or equivalent CTA) on detail page

HTML

* ESC key closes modal

**RESPONSIVE DESIGN REQUIREMENTS**

**Breakpoints**

* Mobile: < 640px
* Tablet: 640px - 1023px
* Desktop: â‰¥ 1024px

**Layout Adjustments**

**Marketplace Page:**

* Filter panel: Drawer on mobile, fixed sidebar on desktop
* Tab navigation: Horizontal scroll on mobile
* Card grid: 1 col (mobile), 2 cols (tablet), 3 cols (desktop)

**Detail Page:**

* Two-column layout becomes single column on mobile
* Sidebar moves below main content on mobile
* Content tabs scroll horizontally on mobile
* Related offerings: 1 col (mobile), 3 cols (desktop)

**Modal:**

* Full screen on small mobile
* Centered modal on tablet/desktop

```html
<Icon name="Library" size={20} />

<span>Library</span>

<span className="tab-count">18</span>

</button>

</nav>

```

\*\*Styling:\*\* Same as Learning Center tabs

- Testimonials: "Search testimonials, organizations, or outcomes..."

- Playbooks: "Search playbooks, industries, or use cases..."

- Library: "Search documents, topics, or authors..."

## BEST PRACTICE CARD COMPONENT

```html

<div className="best-practice-card" onClick={() => navigate(`/marketplaces/knowledge-center/best-practices/${practice.id}`)}>

<div className="card-header">

<div className="card-icon-wrapper">

<Icon name="CheckCircle" className="text-green-600" size={32} />

</div>

{practice.featured && (

<span className="featured-badge">Featured</span>

)}

</div>

<div className="card-content">

<div className="tags-row">

<span className="domain-tag">{practice.domain}</span>

<span className="complexity-badge">{practice.complexity}</span>

</div>

<h3 className="card-title">{practice.title}</h3>

<p className="card-description">{practice.summary}</p>

<div className="card-metadata">

<span className="meta-item">

<Icon name="Layers" size={14} />

{practice.category}

</span>

<span className="meta-item">

<Icon name="TrendingUp" size={14} />

{practice.maturityLevel}

</span>

</div>

<div className="card-footer">

<div className="impact-indicators">

{practice.impactAreas.slice(0, 3).map(area => (

<span className="impact-tag">{area}</span>

))}

</div>

<Icon name="ArrowRight" size={16} className="arrow-icon" />

</div>

</div>

</div>

```

\*\*Card Styling:\*\*

- Similar to Learning Center course card

- Card icon wrapper: w-16 h-16 rounded-lg bg-green-50 flex items-center justify-center mb-4

- Domain tag: bg-blue-100 text-blue-700 px-2 py-1 rounded text-xs font-medium

- Complexity badge: varies by level

- Low: bg-green-100 text-green-700

- Medium: bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-700

- High: bg-red-100 text-red-700

- Impact indicators: flex flex-wrap gap-2 mt-3

- Impact tag: bg-purple-50 text-purple-700 px-2 py-1 rounded text-xs

- Arrow icon: text-orange-600

## LIBRARY ITEM CARD COMPONENT

```html

<div className="library-card" onClick={() => navigate(`/marketplaces/knowledge-center/library/${item.id}`)}>

<div className="library-icon-wrapper">

<Icon name={item.typeIcon} className="library-icon" size={40} />

<span className="format-badge">{item.format}</span>

</div>

<div className="card-content">

<div className="content-type-tag">{item.contentType}</div>

<h3 className="card-title">{item.title}</h3>

<p className="card-description">{item.description}</p>

<div className="library-metadata">

<span className="meta-item">

<Icon name="User" size={14} />

{item.author}

</span>

<span className="meta-item">

<Icon name="FileText" size={14} />

{item.length}

</span>

<span className="meta-item">

<Icon name="Calendar" size={14} />

{item.datePublished}

</span>

</div>

<div className="topics-row">

{item.topics.slice(0, 3).map(topic => (

<span className="topic-tag">{topic}</span>

))}

{item.topics.length > 3 && (

<span className="more-topics">+{item.topics.length - 3}</span>

)}

</div>

<div className="card-footer">

<span className="audience-badge">{item.audience}</span>

<button className="download-btn">

<Icon name="Download" size={16} />

<span>Access</span>

</button>

</div>

</div>

</div>

```

\*\*Library Card Styling:\*\*

- Library icon wrapper: flex items-center justify-between mb-4

- Library icon: text-blue-600

- Format badge: bg-gray-100 text-gray-700 px-2 py-1 rounded text-xs font-medium

- Content type tag: bg-purple-100 text-purple-700 px-2 py-1 rounded text-xs font-semibold inline-block mb-2

- Library metadata: flex flex-wrap items-center gap-3 text-xs text-gray-600 mb-3

- Topics row: flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-4

- Topic tag: bg-blue-50 text-blue-700 px-2 py-1 rounded text-xs

- More topics: text-xs text-gray-500

- Audience badge: bg-orange-100 text-orange-700 px-2 py-1 rounded text-xs font-medium

- Download btn: flex items-center gap-1 text-orange-600 hover:text-orange-700 font-medium text-sm

1. \*\*About\*\* - Overview, key insights, applicability

## SAMPLE DETAIL DATA: API-First Architecture (Best Practice)

```javascript

const bestPracticeDetail = {

id: "api-first-architecture",

title: "API-First Architecture Pattern",

domain: "Architecture",

category: "Architecture",

maturityLevel: "Advanced",

complexity: "Medium",

impactAreas: ["Integration", "Scalability", "Flexibility"],

industryApplicability: "Universal",

contentType: "Pattern",

// About Tab

introduction: "API-First Architecture is a design approach where APIs are treated as first-class citizens in the development process. Rather than building applications first and then exposing APIs as an afterthought, the API-First approach begins with API design, ensuring that all digital capabilities are accessible, reusable, and composable from the start.",

keyInsights: [

"APIs become the contract between systems, enabling parallel development",

"Promotes reusability across web, mobile, and partner integrations",

"Facilitates ecosystem development and partner onboarding",

"Enables faster time-to-market through component reuse",

"Improves system decoupling and independent scalability"

],

whenToApply: "Apply API-First architecture when building digital platforms that will serve multiple channels (web, mobile, IoT), when planning to create partner ecosystems, or when modernizing legacy systems through gradual service extraction.",

// Eligibility Tab

applicability: "This pattern is applicable across all industries and organization sizes. It's particularly valuable for organizations with multi-channel customer engagement, those building platform businesses, or enterprises undergoing digital transformation.",

prerequisites: [

"Basic understanding of RESTful API concepts",

"Familiarity with API design principles",

"Understanding of microservices architecture",

"API management platform or tooling",

"Cross-functional team collaboration capability"

],

bestFor: [

"Enterprise Architects designing platform architectures",

"Solution Architects building multi-channel solutions",

"Product Teams developing new digital products",

"Integration Teams managing system interoperability"

],

// Process Tab

implementationSteps: [

{

title: "API Design First",

description: "Begin with API contract design using OpenAPI/Swagger specifications before writing any code. Involve consumers in the design process."

},

{

title: "Establish API Standards",

description: "Define organizational API standards covering naming conventions, versioning, error handling, security, and documentation."

},

{

title: "Mock and Test",

description: "Create mock servers from API specifications to enable parallel development and early testing by consumers."

},

{

title: "Implement with Contract",

description: "Build backend services to fulfill the API contract, using contract testing to ensure compliance."

},

{

title: "Manage and Monitor",

description: "Deploy APIs through an API gateway, implement rate limiting, and establish monitoring for usage and performance."

},

{

title: "Version and Evolve",

description: "Manage API versions carefully, maintain backward compatibility, and deprecate old versions with proper communication."

}

],

commonPitfalls: [

"Designing APIs without consumer input",

"Insufficient documentation and developer experience",

"Lack of versioning strategy",

"Over-engineering API granularity",

"Inadequate security and access control"

],

// Documents Tab

relatedDocuments: [

{ name: "API Design Guidelines", type: "PDF", size: "2.1 MB" },

{ name: "OpenAPI Specification Template", type: "YAML", size: "0.3 MB" },

{ name: "API Governance Framework", type: "PDF", size: "1.8 MB" }

],

relatedResources: [

"API Management Platform Setup Guide",

"Contract Testing Best Practices",

"API Security Checklist"

]

}
```

## Templates Marketplace

# TEMPLATES MARKETPLACE

This is \*\*Prompt 4 of 9\*\* in building the complete DTMP v3 platform.

\*\*Already Built:\*\*

- Prompt 1: Foundation (Header, Footer, Landing, Marketplaces Overview, Design System)

- Prompt 2: Learning Center (complete marketplace with tabs, filters, detail pages, login modal, Stage 2)

- Prompt 3: Knowledge Center (4 tabs: Best Practices, Testimonials, Playbooks, Library)

\*\*Building in this prompt:\*\*

- Complete Templates marketplace page with 6 tabs

- Tab-based navigation (Policy Reports, Procedure Reports, Application Profiles, Strategy Docs, Assessments, Executive Summaries)

- Left filter panel (tab-specific filters)

- Global search bar (marketplace-scoped)

- Service card grids (70+ template cards total across 6 tabs)

- Detail page component (reusing structure, with Templates-specific content)

- Template preview and customization UI elements

- Reuse login modal and Stage 2 placeholder

\*\*Key Differentiator:\*\*

Templates marketplace emphasizes AI-powered generation (DocWriter 4.0), template customization, and document output formats.

## TECHNICAL STACK

Same as previous prompts:

- React with TypeScript

- React Router v6

- Tailwind CSS

- Lucide React icons

- Responsive mobile-first design

## TEMPLATE CARD COMPONENT (Universal for all tabs)

```html

<div className="template-card" onClick={() => navigate(`/marketplaces/templates/${tab}/${template.id}`)}>

<div className="card-header">

<div className="template-icon-wrapper">

<Icon name={template.icon} className="template-icon" size={32} />

</div>

<span>{template.aiGeneration}</span>

</div>

</div>

<div className="card-content">

<div className="template-tags">

<span className="category-tag">{template.category}</span>

{template.compliance && (

<span className="compliance-badge">

<Icon name="ShieldCheck" size={12} />

{template.compliance}

</span>

)}

</div>

<h3 className="card-title">{template.title}</h3>

<p className="card-description">{template.description}</p>

<div className="template-features">

<div className="feature-item">

<Icon name="FileText" size={14} />

<span>{template.pageLength}</span>

</div>

<div className="feature-item">

<Icon name="Download" size={14} />

<span>{template.outputFormats.join(', ')}</span>

</div>

{template.specialFeature && (

<div className="feature-item">

<Icon name="Star" size={14} />

<span>{template.specialFeature}</span>

</div>

)}

</div>

<div className="card-footer">

<span className="usage-count">

<Icon name="Users" size={14} />

{template.usageCount} uses

</span>

<button className="generate-btn">

<Icon name="Wand2" size={16} />

Generate

</button>

</div>

</div>

</div>

```

- Rounded: rounded-xl

- Text: text-white

- Display: inline-flex items-center gap-3

- Shadow: shadow-lg

- Animation: subtle shimmer effect on background

- Complete Templates marketplace with 70 total template cards

- All 6 tabs functional with appropriate filters

- AI DocWriter 4.0 branding prominent

- Detail pages show template-specific content (customization, AI features, etc.)

## Blueprints marketplace

This is \*\*Prompt 5 of 9\*\* in building the complete DTMP v3 platform.

\*\*Already Built:\*\*

- Prompt 1: Foundation (Header, Footer, Landing, Marketplaces Overview, Design System)

- Prompt 2: Learning Center (Courses, Learning Tracks, Reviews)

- Prompt 3: Knowledge Center (Best Practices, Testimonials, Playbooks, Library)

- Prompt 4: Templates (6 tabs with 70+ templates, AI DocWriter 4.0)

\*\*Building in this prompt:\*\*

- Complete Blueprints marketplace page with 2 tabs

- Tab-based navigation (Solution Specs, Solution Build)

- Left filter panel (tab-specific filters)

- Global search bar (marketplace-scoped)

- Service card grids (25 solution specs, 14 solution builds)

- Detail page component (reusing structure, with Blueprints-specific content)

- Technical architecture diagrams and component lists

- Reuse login modal and Stage 2 placeholder

\*\*Key Differentiator:\*\*

Blueprints marketplace serves BOTH Design phase (Solution Specs) and Deploy phase (Solution Build), featuring technical architecture blueprints for building digital platforms.

## TECHNICAL STACK

Same as previous prompts:

- React with TypeScript

- React Router v6

- Tailwind CSS

- Lucide React icons

- Responsive mobile-first design

## MARKETPLACE HEADER

```html

<section className="marketplace-header">

<nav className="breadcrumb">

<a href="/">Home</a>

<span className="separator">/</span>

<a href="/marketplaces">Marketplaces</a>

<span className="separator">/</span>

<span className="current">Blueprints</span>

</nav>

<div className="header-content">

<div className="dual-phase-badges">

<span className="phase-badge design">Design</span>

<span className="phase-separator">+</span>

<span className="phase-badge deploy">Deploy</span>

</div>

<h1 className="marketplace-title">DTMP Blueprints</h1>

<p className="marketplace-description">

Comprehensive solution specifications and build guides for digital

platforms. Access detailed architecture blueprints for DBP, DXP, DWS,

DIA, and SecDevOps solutions. Design phase provides specifications and

architecture; Deploy phase provides implementation guides and patterns.

</p>

<div className="marketplace-stats">

<span className="stat">

<Icon name="FileText" size={18} />

39 Total Blueprints

</span>

<span className="stat">

<Icon name="Layout" size={18} />

Architecture Diagrams

</span>

<span className="stat">

<Icon name="Code" size={18} />

Implementation Guides

</span>

</div>

</div>

</section>

```

\*\*Dual Phase Badges Styling:\*\*

- Container: flex items-center gap-2 mb-3

- Phase badges: same styling as previous (bg-purple-100 text-purple-700 for Design, bg-green-100 text-green-700 for Deploy)

- Phase separator: text-gray-400 font-bold text-lg

## FEATURE TABS

```html
</button>

</nav>

```

- Background: inline badge

- Design: bg-purple-100 text-purple-700

- Deploy: bg-green-100 text-green-700

- Padding: px-2 py-0.5

- Rounded: rounded

- Font: text-xs font-semibold

- Position: ml-2

\*\*Mobile Tab Labels (shortened):\*\*

- Blueprint-led Solution Specs â†’ "Solution Specs"

- Solutions Blueprints Build â†’ "Solution Build"

## GLOBAL SEARCH BAR

- Solution Specs: "Search solution blueprints or platforms..."

- Solution Build: "Search implementation guides or technologies..."

## FILTER GROUPS BY TAB

#### \*\*SOLUTION SPECS TAB FILTERS:\*\*

```javascript

const solutionSpecsFilters = {

solutionType: ["DBP - Digital Business Platform", "DXP - Digital Experience Platform", "DWS - Digital Workspace Solutions", "DIA - Data, Intelligence & Analytics", "SDO - Secure DevOps Operations"],

blueprintScope: ["Enterprise Reference Architecture", "Domain Architecture", "Solution Architecture", "Component Architecture"],

maturityLevel: ["Foundation", "Intermediate", "Advanced", "Leading Edge"],

industryFocus: ["Cross-Industry", "Financial Services", "Healthcare", "Retail", "Manufacturing", "Public Sector"],

technicalComplexity: ["Low", "Medium", "High", "Very High"],

deploymentModel: ["Cloud-Native", "Hybrid", "On-Premise", "Multi-Cloud"],

includesDiagrams: ["Yes - Comprehensive", "Yes - Basic", "No"],

includesComponentList: ["Yes", "No"]

}

```

#### \*\*SOLUTION BUILD TAB FILTERS:\*\*

```javascript

const solutionBuildFilters = {

solutionType: ["DBP Platform", "DXP Platform", "DWS Platform", "DIA Platform", "SDO Platform"],

implementationTime: ["< 1 month", "1-3 months", "3-6 months", "6+ months"],

skillLevel: ["Beginner", "Intermediate", "Advanced", "Expert"]

}

```

## BLUEPRINT CARD COMPONENT (Universal for both tabs)

```html

<div className="blueprint-card" onClick={() => navigate(`/marketplaces/blueprints/${tab}/${blueprint.id}`)}>

<div className="card-header">

<div className="blueprint-icon-wrapper">

<Icon name={blueprint.icon} className="blueprint-icon" size={36} />

</div>

<div className="blueprint-badges">

<span className="solution-type-badge">{blueprint.solutionTypeShort}</span>

{blueprint.featured && (

<span className="featured-star">

<Icon name="Star" size={14} />

</span>

)}

</div>

</div>

<div className="card-content">

<h3 className="card-title">{blueprint.title}</h3>

<p className="card-description">{blueprint.description}</p>

<div className="blueprint-features">

<div className="feature-row">

<Icon name="Layers" size={14} />

<span>{blueprint.scope}</span>

</div>

<div className="feature-row">

<Icon name="TrendingUp" size={14} />

<span>{blueprint.maturityLevel}</span>

</div>

{blueprint.includesDiagrams && (

<div className="feature-row">

<Icon name="GitBranch" size={14} />

<span>Architecture Diagrams</span>

</div>

)}

{blueprint.includesComponents && (

<div className="feature-row">

<Icon name="Package" size={14} />

<span>{blueprint.componentCount} Components</span>

</div>

)}

</div>

<div className="tech-stack-row">

{blueprint.keyTechnologies.slice(0, 3).map(tech => (

<span className="tech-tag">{tech}</span>

))}

{blueprint.keyTechnologies.length > 3 && (

<span className="more-tech">+{blueprint.keyTechnologies.length - 3}</span>

)}

</div>

<div className="card-footer">

<span className="complexity-badge complexity-{blueprint.complexity.toLowerCase()}">

{blueprint.complexity}

</span>

<button className="view-blueprint-btn">

<Icon name="Eye" size={16} />

View Blueprint

</button>

</div>

</div>

</div>

```

\*\*Blueprint Card Styling:\*\*

- Background: bg-white

- Border: border-2 border-gray-200

- Rounded: rounded-xl

- Padding: p-6

- Hover: hover:border-blue-500 hover:shadow-2xl hover:-translate-y-1 transition-all duration-300

- Cursor: cursor-pointer

\*\*Card Header:\*\*

- Flex: flex justify-between items-start mb-4

\*\*Blueprint Icon Wrapper:\*\*

- Size: w-20 h-20

- Background: bg-gradient-to-br from-blue-100 to-indigo-100

- Rounded: rounded-xl

- Flex: flex items-center justify-center

\*\*Blueprint Icon:\*\*

- Color: text-blue-600

\*\*Blueprint Badges:\*\*

- Flex: flex items-center gap-2

\*\*Solution Type Badge:\*\*

- Background: varies by type

- DBP: bg-purple-100 text-purple-700

- DXP: bg-pink-100 text-pink-700

- DWS: bg-blue-100 text-blue-700

- DIA: bg-green-100 text-green-700

- SDO: bg-orange-100 text-orange-700

- Padding: px-3 py-1

- Rounded: rounded-full

- Font: text-xs font-bold uppercase

\*\*Featured Star:\*\*

- Color: text-yellow-500 fill-yellow-500

\*\*Blueprint Features:\*\*

- Background: bg-gray-50

- Border: border border-gray-200

- Rounded: rounded-lg

- Padding: p-4

- Space: space-y-2

- Margin: mb-4

\*\*Feature Row:\*\*

- Flex: flex items-center gap-2

- Font: text-sm text-gray-700

\*\*Tech Stack Row:\*\*

- Flex: flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-4

\*\*Tech Tag:\*\*

- Background: bg-blue-50 border border-blue-200

- Text: text-blue-700

- Padding: px-2 py-1

- Rounded: rounded

- Font: text-xs font-medium

\*\*More Tech:\*\*

- Font: text-xs text-gray-500

\*\*Complexity Badge:\*\*

- Padding: px-3 py-1

- Rounded: rounded-full

- Font: text-xs font-semibold

- Colors by complexity:

- Low: bg-green-100 text-green-700

- Medium: bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-700

- High: bg-orange-100 text-orange-700

- Very High: bg-red-100 text-red-700

\*\*View Blueprint Button:\*\*

- Background: bg-blue-600 text-white hover:bg-blue-700

- Padding: px-4 py-2

- Rounded: rounded-lg

- Font: text-sm font-semibold

- Flex: flex items-center gap-2

## DETAIL PAGE CONTENT

\*\*Reuse detail page structure with Blueprints-specific content.\*\*

### Content Tabs for Blueprints:

1. \*\*About\*\* - Blueprint overview, architecture philosophy, use cases

2. \*\*Architecture\*\* - Technical architecture, diagrams, component descriptions

3. \*\*Components\*\* - Detailed component list with specifications

4. \*\*Implementation\*\* - Implementation guidance, prerequisites, steps

5. \*\*Resources\*\* - Related documents, tools, references

## SAMPLE DETAIL DATA: DBP Reference Architecture

## RESPONSIVE & ACCESSIBILITY

Same requirements as previous marketplaces:

â€¢ Mobile-first responsive design

â€¢ Filter panel: drawer on mobile, sidebar on desktop

â€¢ Tab navigation: horizontal scroll on mobile (2 tabs)

â€¢ Card grids: 1 col (mobile), 2 cols (tablet), 3 cols (desktop)

â€¢ All WCAG AA accessibility standards

â€¢ Dual phase badges stack on mobile, inline on desktop

Mobile-Specific Adjustments:

â€¢ Blueprint icon wrapper: smaller on mobile (w-16 h-16 vs w-20 h-20)

â€¢ Technology tags: max 2 visible on mobile, "+X" for remaining

â€¢ Component count displayed abbreviated on mobile

## UNIQUE BLUEPRINT FEATURES

Architecture Diagram Viewer (Optional Enhancement)

Display diagrams in detail page Architecture tab:

```html

<div className="diagram-viewer">

<div className="diagram-tabs">

{architectureDiagrams.map(diagram => (

<button className={`diagram-tab ${activeDiagram === diagram.name ? 'active' : ''}`}>

{diagram.name}

</button>

))}

</div>

<div className="diagram-display">

<div className="diagram-placeholder">

<Icon name="Layout" size={64} className="text-gray-400" />

<p className="diagram-title">{activeDiagram.name}</p>

<p className="diagram-description">{activeDiagram.description}</p>

<div className="diagram-actions">

<button className="download-diagram-btn">

<Icon name="Download" size={16} />

Download

</button>

<button className="fullscreen-btn">

<Icon name="Maximize2" size={16} />

View Fullscreen

</button>

</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

```

Diagram Viewer Styling:

â€¢ Container: border border-gray-300 rounded-lg overflow-hidden

â€¢ Diagram tabs: flex overflow-x-auto border-b border-gray-300 bg-gray-50

â€¢ Diagram tab: px-4 py-3 text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 hover:bg-white transition-colors

â€¢ Active diagram tab: bg-white border-b-2 border-blue-600 text-blue-600

â€¢ Diagram display: aspect-video bg-gray-100 flex items-center justify-center p-8

â€¢ Diagram placeholder: text-center space-y-4

â€¢ Diagram title: text-xl font-semibold text-gray-900

â€¢ Diagram description: text-sm text-gray-600 max-w-md mx-auto

â€¢ Diagram actions: flex gap-3 justify-center mt-6

â€¢ Download/fullscreen buttons: bg-white border border-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-50 px-4 py-2 rounded-lg text-sm font-medium flex items-center gap-2

Note: Actual diagram images would be stored as SVG or PNG files. Placeholder shows conceptual UI.

Component List Table

Display components in detail page Components tab:

```html

<div className="components-table-container">

<div className="table-header">

<h3 className="table-title">Architecture Components</h3>

<div className="table-filters">

<select className="category-filter">

<option>All Categories</option>

<option>Integration</option>

<option>Security</option>

<option>Data</option>

<option>Experience</option>

</select>

<input

type="text"

placeholder="Search components..."

className="component-search"

/>

</div>

</div>

<div className="table-responsive">

<table className="components-table">

<thead>

<tr>

<th>Component</th>

<th>Category</th>

<th>Key Capabilities</th>

<th>Technologies</th>

<th>Interfaces</th>

</tr>

</thead>

<tbody>

{components.map(component => (

<tr className="component-row">

<td className="component-name-cell">

<Icon name={component.icon || "Box"} size={20} className="text-blue-600" />

<div>

<p className="component-name">{component.name}</p>

<p className="component-desc">{component.description}</p>

</div>

</td>

<td>

<span className="category-badge">{component.category}</span>

</td>

<td>

<ul className="capabilities-list">

{component.capabilities.slice(0, 3).map(cap => (

<li>{cap}</li>

))}

{component.capabilities.length > 3 && (

<li className="more-capabilities">+{component.capabilities.length - 3} more</li>

)}

</ul>

</td>

<td>

<div className="tech-tags">

{component.technologies.slice(0, 2).map(tech => (

<span className="tech-tag-small">{tech}</span>

))}

{component.technologies.length > 2 && (

<span className="more-tech-small">+{component.technologies.length - 2}</span>

)}

</div>

</td>

<td>

<div className="interfaces-list">

{component.interfaces.map(intf => (

<span className="interface-badge">{intf}</span>

))}

</div>

</td>

</tr>

))}

</tbody>

</table>

</div>

</div>

```

Components Table Styling:

â€¢ Container: bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-xl overflow-hidden

â€¢ Table header: flex justify-between items-center p-6 border-b border-gray-200

â€¢ Table title: text-xl font-bold text-gray-900

â€¢ Table filters: flex gap-3

â€¢ Category filter: border border-gray-300 rounded-lg px-3 py-2 text-sm

â€¢ Component search: border border-gray-300 rounded-lg px-3 py-2 text-sm w-64

â€¢ Table responsive: overflow-x-auto

â€¢ Components table: w-full text-sm

â€¢ Table header: bg-gray-50 border-b border-gray-200

â€¢ Table th: text-left px-4 py-3 font-semibold text-gray-700 uppercase text-xs

â€¢ Component row: border-b border-gray-100 hover:bg-gray-50 transition-colors

â€¢ Table td: px-4 py-4

â€¢ Component name cell: flex items-start gap-3

â€¢ Component name: font-semibold text-gray-900

â€¢ Component desc: text-xs text-gray-600 mt-1

â€¢ Category badge: bg-blue-100 text-blue-700 px-2 py-1 rounded text-xs font-medium

â€¢ Capabilities list: list-disc list-inside space-y-1 text-xs text-gray-600

â€¢ More capabilities: text-blue-600 font-medium

â€¢ Tech tags: flex flex-wrap gap-1

â€¢ Tech tag small: bg-gray-100 text-gray-700 px-2 py-1 rounded text-xs

â€¢ More tech small: text-xs text-gray-500

â€¢ Interface badge: bg-green-100 text-green-700 px-2 py-1 rounded text-xs font-medium

Mobile Table:

â€¢ Convert to card view on mobile

Implementation Timeline Visualization

Display implementation phases in detail page Implementation tab:

```html

<div className="implementation-timeline">

<h3 className="timeline-title">Implementation Roadmap</h3>

<div className="timeline-container">

{implementationPhases.map((phase, index) => (

<div className="timeline-phase">

<div className="phase-connector">

<div className="phase-dot"></div>

{index < implementationPhases.length - 1 && (

<div className="phase-line"></div>

)}

</div>

<div className="phase-content">

<div className="phase-header">

<span className="phase-number">Phase {index + 1}</span>

<h4 className="phase-title">{phase.phase}</h4>

</div>

<p className="phase-focus">

<strong>Focus:</strong> {phase.focus}

</p>

<div className="phase-deliverables">

<p className="deliverables-label">Key Deliverables:</p>

<ul className="deliverables-list">

{phase.deliverables.map(deliverable => (

<li>{deliverable}</li>

))}

</ul>

</div>

</div>

</div>

))}

</div>

</div>

```

\*\*Implementation Timeline Styling:\*\*

- Timeline title: text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900 mb-8

- Timeline container: space-y-8

- Timeline phase: flex gap-6

- Phase connector: flex flex-col items-center flex-shrink-0

```html
)}

</div>
```

**Content Tabs for Portfolio Management:**

1. **About** - Service overview, objectives, value proposition
2. **Methodology** - Analysis approach, frameworks used, data sources

Same requirements as previous marketplaces:

* Mobile-first responsive design
* Filter panel: drawer on mobile, sidebar on desktop
* Tab navigation: horizontal scroll on mobile (2 tabs)
* Card grids: 1 col (mobile), 2 cols (tablet), 3 cols (desktop)
* All WCAG AA accessibility standards

**Mobile-Specific Adjustments:**

* Health scorecard: single column on mobile
* Methodology framework: single column on mobile
* Metric values: slightly smaller font size on mobile
* Dashboard preview images: full-width on mobile

\*\*Building in this prompt:\*\*

- Tab-based navigation (Systems Portfolio & Lifecycle, Digital Maturity, Projects Portfolio & Lifecycle)

- Left filter panel (tab-specific filters)

\*\*Key Differentiator:\*\*

### FILTER GROUPS BY TAB

### INTELLIGENCE SERVICE CARD COMPONENT (Universal for all tabs)

```html

<div className="intelligence-card" onClick={() => navigate(`/marketplaces/digital-intelligence/${tab}/${service.id}`)}>

<div className="card-header">

<div className="service-icon-wrapper">

<Icon name={service.icon} className="service-icon" size={32} />

</div>

<div className="service-badges">

<span className="analytics-badge">{service.analyticsType}</span>

{service.aiPowered && (

<span className="ai-badge">

<Icon name="Brain" size={12} />

AI

</span>

)}

</div>

</div>

<div className="card-content">

<h3 className="card-title">{service.title}</h3>

<p className="card-description">{service.description}</p>

<div className="service-capabilities">

<p className="capabilities-label">AI Capabilities:</p>

<div className="capabilities-list">

{service.aiCapabilities.slice(0, 2).map(capability => (

<span className="capability-tag">

<Icon name="Sparkles" size={12} />

{capability}

</span>

))}

</div>

</div>

<div className="service-features">

<div className="feature-item">

<Icon name="Database" size={14} />

<span>{service.dataSource}</span>

</div>

<div className="feature-item">

<Icon name="RefreshCw" size={14} />

<span>{service.updateFrequency}</span>

</div>

<div className="feature-item">

<Icon name="BarChart3" size={14} />

<span>{service.visualizationType}</span>

</div>

</div>

{service.keyInsights && (

<div className="key-insights">

<p className="insights-label">Key Insights:</p>

<div className="insights-list">

{service.keyInsights.slice(0, 2).map(insight => (

<span className="insight-tag">{insight}</span>

))}

</div>

</div>

)}

<div className="card-footer">

<span className="accuracy-indicator">

<Icon name="Target" size={14} />

{service.accuracy || 'High Accuracy'}

</span>

<button className="access-analytics-btn">

<Icon name="BarChart3" size={16} />

View Analytics

</button>

</div>

</div>

</div>

```

\*\*Intelligence Card Styling:\*\*

- Background: bg-white

- Border: border-2 border-gray-200

- Rounded: rounded-xl

- Padding: p-6

- Hover: hover:border-purple-500 hover:shadow-2xl hover:-translate-y-1 transition-all duration-300

- Cursor: cursor-pointer

\*\*Card Header:\*\*

- Flex: flex justify-between items-start mb-4

\*\*Service Icon Wrapper:\*\*

- Size: w-16 h-16

- Background: bg-gradient-to-br from-purple-100 to-pink-100

- Rounded: rounded-xl

- Flex: flex items-center justify-center

\*\*Service Icon:\*\*

- Color: text-purple-600

\*\*Service Badges:\*\*

- Flex: flex items-center gap-2

\*\*Analytics Badge:\*\*

- Background: bg-blue-100 text-blue-700

- Padding: px-3 py-1

- Rounded: rounded-full

- Font: text-xs font-semibold uppercase

\*\*AI Badge:\*\*

- Background: bg-gradient-to-r from-purple-600 to-pink-600 text-white

- Padding: px-2 py-1

- Rounded: rounded-full

- Font: text-xs font-bold

- Flex: flex items-center gap-1

- Shadow: shadow-md

\*\*Service Capabilities:\*\*

- Border: border-l-4 border-purple-500

- Background: bg-purple-50

- Padding: p-3

- Rounded: rounded-r-lg

- Margin: mb-4

\*\*Capabilities Label:\*\*

- Font: text-xs font-semibold text-purple-700 uppercase mb-2

\*\*Capabilities List:\*\*

- Flex: flex flex-wrap gap-2

\*\*Capability Tag:\*\*

- Background: bg-white border border-purple-200

- Text: text-purple-700

- Padding: px-2 py-1

- Rounded: rounded

- Font: text-xs font-medium

- Flex: flex items-center gap-1

\*\*Service Features:\*\*

- Background: bg-gray-50

- Border: border border-gray-200

- Rounded: rounded-lg

- Padding: p-3

- Space: space-y-2

- Margin: mb-4

\*\*Feature Item:\*\*

- Flex: flex items-center gap-2

- Font: text-sm text-gray-700

\*\*Key Insights:\*\*

- Border top: border-t border-gray-200 pt-3 mb-4

\*\*Insights Label:\*\*

- Font: text-xs font-semibold text-gray-700 uppercase mb-2

\*\*Insights List:\*\*

- Flex: flex flex-wrap gap-2

\*\*Insight Tag:\*\*

- Background: bg-green-50 text-green-700

- Border: border border-green-200

- Padding: px-2 py-1

- Rounded: rounded

- Font: text-xs font-medium

\*\*Card Footer:\*\*

- Flex: flex justify-between items-center

- Border top: border-t border-gray-200 pt-4

\*\*Accuracy Indicator:\*\*

- Font: text-sm text-gray-600

- Flex: flex items-center gap-1

\*\*Access Analytics Button:\*\*

- Background: bg-purple-600 text-white hover:bg-purple-700

- Padding: px-4 py-2

- Rounded: rounded-lg

**DETAIL PAGE CONTENT**

**Reuse detail page structure with Digital Intelligence-specific content.**

**Content Tabs for Digital Intelligence:**

1. **About** - Service overview, AI capabilities, value proposition
2. **AI Model** - Machine learning model details, training data, accuracy metrics
3. **Insights & Outputs** - What insights are provided, visualization types, sample outputs
4. **Data & Integration** - Data sources, integration requirements, data quality needs
5. **Getting Started** - Access setup, configuration, training resources

**SAMPLE DETAIL DATA: Predictive Maintenance Intelligence**

javascript

const predictiveMaintenanceDetail = {

id: "predictive-maintenance",

title: "Predictive Maintenance Intelligence",

analyticsType: "Predictive Analytics",

systemScope: "Enterprise-wide",

aiPowered: true,

updateFrequency: "Hourly",

*// About Tab*

overview: "Predictive Maintenance Intelligence leverages advanced machine learning algorithms to predict system failures and maintenance needs before they occur. By analyzing historical incident data, performance metrics, and environmental factors, the AI model identifies patterns that precede failures, enabling proactive maintenance scheduling and preventing costly downtime.",

businessValue: [

"Reduce unplanned downtime by 40-60%",

"Decrease maintenance costs by 25-35%",

"Extend system lifespan by 15-20%",

"Improve resource utilization and planning",

"Prevent cascading failures across integrated systems"

],

keyCapabilities: [

"Failure prediction 3-14 days in advance",

"Maintenance window optimization",

"Root cause identification",

"Cost-benefit analysis of maintenance actions",

"Automated alert generation with recommended actions"

],

useCases: [

"Critical infrastructure monitoring (servers, networks, storage)",

"Business-critical application monitoring",

"IoT and industrial equipment management",

"Database and data platform health",

"Integration middleware and API gateway health"

],

whoShouldUse: [

"IT Operations teams managing critical infrastructure",

"Platform Engineering teams",

"Database Administrators",

"Enterprise Architects planning capacity",

"Service Delivery Managers responsible for uptime SLAs"

],

*// AI Model Tab*

modelArchitecture: "The predictive maintenance model uses an ensemble approach combining Random Forest, Gradient Boosting, and LSTM (Long Short-Term Memory) neural networks. This hybrid architecture captures both structured patterns in system metrics and temporal sequences in time-series data.",

trainingData: {

description: "The model is trained on 3+ years of historical data from production environments",

dataPoints: [

"System performance metrics (CPU, memory, disk I/O, network)",

"Application logs and error patterns",

"Historical incident and maintenance records",

"Configuration changes and deployment events",

"Environmental data (load patterns, user activity)",

"Dependency and integration health metrics"

],

dataVolume: "500+ million data points across 2,000+ systems",

updateFrequency: "Model retrained monthly with new data"

},

accuracyMetrics: {

failurePrediction: "88% accuracy (validated against last 12 months)",

falsePositiveRate: "12% (continuously improving)",

leadTime: "Average 7-day advance warning",

precisionRecall: {

precision: "85%",

recall: "88%",

f1Score: "86.5%"

}

},

predictionProcess: [

* Model accuracy grid: single column on mobile

* Mobile experience excellent for data/analytics content
* AI capabilities emphasized throughout

Build the Digital Intelligence marketplace emphasizing AI-powered analytics, predictive insights, automated maturity assessments, and data-driven intelligence for continuous improvement in the Drive phase.

Create the DTMP Support Services marketplace - the final marketplace providing technical support and expert consultancy in the Drive phase.

---

## Support Services marketplace

This is \*\*Prompt 8 of 9\*\* in building the complete DTMP v3 platform.

\*\*Already Built:\*\*

- Prompt 1: Foundation (Header, Footer, Landing, Marketplaces Overview, Design System)

- Prompt 2: Learning Center (Courses, Learning Tracks, Reviews) - Discern

- Prompt 3: Knowledge Center (Best Practices, Testimonials, Playbooks, Library) - Discern

- Prompt 4: Templates (6 tabs with 70+ templates, AI DocWriter 4.0) - Design

- Prompt 5: Blueprints (Solution Specs, Solution Build, 39 blueprints) - Design + Deploy

- Prompt 6: Portfolio Management (Application Portfolio, Project Portfolio, 32 services) - Drive

- Prompt 7: Digital Intelligence (Systems, Maturity, Projects, 30 services) - Drive

\*\*Building in this prompt:\*\*

- Complete Support Services marketplace page with 2 tabs

- Tab-based navigation (Technical Support, Expert Consultancy)

- Left filter panel (tab-specific filters)

- Global search bar (marketplace-scoped)

- Service card grids (18 technical support services, 16 consultancy services)

- Detail page component (reusing structure, with Support Services-specific content)

- SLA tiers, response times, and expert profiles emphasis

- Reuse login modal and Stage 2 placeholder

\*\*Key Differentiator:\*\*

Support Services marketplace focuses on human expertise, responsive technical support, specialized consultancy, and expert guidance for transformation challenges in the Drive phase.

Same as previous prompts:

- React with TypeScript

- React Router v6

- Tailwind CSS

- Lucide React icons

- Responsive mobile-first design

## ROUTING

\*\*New routes for this prompt:\*\*

```javascript

// Support Services marketplace

{ path: '/marketplaces/support-services', element: <SupportServicesPage /> }

// Detail pages (dynamic route)

{ path: '/marketplaces/support-services/:tab/:cardId', element: <DetailPage /> }

```

\*\*Example detail page URLs:\*\*

- `/marketplaces/support-services/technical-support/24x7-platform-support`

- `/marketplaces/support-services/technical-support/incident-response`

- `/marketplaces/support-services/expert-consultancy/architecture-advisory`

- `/marketplaces/support-services/expert-consultancy/transformation-coaching`

### SUPPORT SERVICE CARD COMPONENT (Universal for both tabs)

```html

<div className="support-card" onClick={() => navigate(`/marketplaces/support-services/${tab}/${service.id}`)}>

<div className="card-header">

<div className="service-icon-wrapper">

<Icon name={service.icon} className="service-icon" size={32} />

</div>

<div className="service-badges">

<span className="type-badge">{service.type}</span>

{service.slaLevel && (

<span className="sla-badge sla-{service.slaLevel.toLowerCase()}">

<Icon name="Clock" size={12} />

{service.slaLevel}

</span>

)}

</div>

</div>

<div className="card-content">

<h3 className="card-title">{service.title}</h3>

<p className="card-description">{service.description}</p>

{service.expertProfile && (

<div className="expert-preview">

<div className="expert-avatar">{service.expertProfile.initials}</div>

<div className="expert-info">

<p className="expert-name">{service.expertProfile.name}</p>

<p className="expert-title">{service.expertProfile.title}</p>

</div>

</div>

)}

<div className="service-features">

<div className="feature-item">

<Icon name="Clock" size={14} />

<span>{service.responseTime || service.duration}</span>

</div>

<div className="feature-item">

<Icon name="MapPin" size={14} />

<span>{service.deliveryModel}</span>

</div>

{service.coverage && (

<div className="feature-item">

<Icon name="Shield" size={14} />

<span>{service.coverage}</span>

</div>

)}

</div>

{service.keyBenefits && (

<div className="key-benefits">

<p className="benefits-label">Key Benefits:</p>

<div className="benefits-list">

{service.keyBenefits.slice(0, 2).map(benefit => (

<span className="benefit-tag">

<Icon name="Check" size={12} />

{benefit}

</span>

))}

</div>

</div>

)}

<div className="card-footer">

<span className="pricing-indicator">

<Icon name="DollarSign" size={14} />

{service.pricing}

</span>

<button className="request-btn">

<Icon name="Send" size={16} />

Request Service

</button>

</div>

</div>

</div>

```

\*\*Support Card Styling:\*\*

- Background: bg-white

- Border: border-2 border-gray-200

- Rounded: rounded-xl

- Padding: p-6

- Hover: hover:border-green-500 hover:shadow-2xl hover:-translate-y-1 transition-all duration-300

- Cursor: cursor-pointer

\*\*Card Header:\*\*

- Flex: flex justify-between items-start mb-4

\*\*Service Icon Wrapper:\*\*

- Size: w-16 h-16

- Background: bg-gradient-to-br from-green-100 to-teal-100

- Rounded: rounded-xl

- Flex: flex items-center justify-center

\*\*Service Icon:\*\*

- Color: text-green-600

\*\*Service Badges:\*\*

- Flex: flex items-center gap-2

\*\*Type Badge:\*\*

- Background: bg-blue-100 text-blue-700

- Padding: px-3 py-1

- Rounded: rounded-full

- Font: text-xs font-semibold uppercase

\*\*SLA Badge:\*\*

- Padding: px-2 py-1

- Rounded: rounded-full

- Font: text-xs font-semibold

- Flex: flex items-center gap-1

- Colors by level:

- Critical: bg-red-100 text-red-700

- High: bg-orange-100 text-orange-700

- Standard: bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-700

- Best Effort: bg-gray-100 text-gray-700

\*\*Expert Preview:\*\*

- Background: bg-gradient-to-r from-purple-50 to-pink-50

- Border: border border-purple-200

- Padding: p-3

- Rounded: rounded-lg

- Flex: flex items-center gap-3

- Margin: mb-4

\*\*Expert Avatar:\*\*

- Size: w-10 h-10

- Background: bg-gradient-to-br from-purple-600 to-pink-600

- Text: text-white font-bold

- Rounded: rounded-full

- Flex: flex items-center justify-center

\*\*Expert Info:\*\*

- Flex: flex-1

\*\*Expert Name:\*\*

- Font: text-sm font-semibold text-gray-900

\*\*Expert Title:\*\*

- Font: text-xs text-gray-600

\*\*Service Features:\*\*

- Background: bg-gray-50

- Border: border border-gray-200

- Rounded: rounded-lg

- Padding: p-3

- Space: space-y-2

- Margin: mb-4

\*\*Feature Item:\*\*

- Flex: flex items-center gap-2

- Font: text-sm text-gray-700

\*\*Key Benefits:\*\*

- Border top: border-t border-gray-200 pt-3 mb-4

\*\*Benefits Label:\*\*

- Font: text-xs font-semibold text-gray-700 uppercase mb-2

\*\*Benefits List:\*\*

- Flex: flex flex-wrap gap-2

\*\*Benefit Tag:\*\*

- Background: bg-green-50 text-green-700

- Border: border border-green-200

- Padding: px-2 py-1

- Rounded: rounded

- Font: text-xs font-medium

- Flex: flex items-center gap-1

\*\*Card Footer:\*\*

- Flex: flex justify-between items-center

- Border top: border-t border-gray-200 pt-4

\*\*Pricing Indicator:\*\*

- Font: text-sm text-gray-600

- Flex: flex items-center gap-1

- Padding: px-4 py-2

- Rounded: rounded-lg

- Flex: flex items-center gap-2

**RESPONSIVE & ACCESSIBILITY**

Same requirements as previous marketplaces:

* Mobile-first responsive design
* Filter panel: drawer on mobile, sidebar on desktop
* Tab navigation: horizontal scroll on mobile (2 tabs)
* Card grids: 1 col (mobile), 2 cols (tablet), 3 cols (desktop)
* All WCAG AA accessibility standards

**Mobile-Specific Adjustments:**

* SLA tiers: single column on mobile
* Expert profile: avatar smaller on mobile, content stacks
* Engagement models: single column on mobile
* Expert preview on card: stack vertically on mobile
